posted:Posted October 6, 2021
msg:I have stayed in five-star hotels on Ctrip many times, and the experience this time was definitely poor. The following is an objective sharing of my thoughts, with pros and cons:
Advantages: 1. Good sound insulation; 2. The style of breakfast and dinner dishes in the cafeteria is acceptable (basically home-cooked dishes + salads + some cold dishes); almost the same combination, but the price is cheaper than other five-star rated restaurants, 68 buffet for dinner, 3. Distance Mizoguchi is not too far, about 4 kilometers, but it is not too close; 4. The decoration feels like a four-star rating or above, which is okay.
shortcoming:
1. In terms of hardware: 1. The water in the bathroom is relatively turbid, and there will be a lot of foam when you use it, and it stays for a long time. I don‚Äôt know what happened; 2. The hotel room is very small. I haven‚Äôt stayed in such a small room at this price in a long time. , even after I ordered a superior twin bed and got a free upgrade to a deluxe twin bed, it still felt small. 3. There is no air conditioning. If you want to cool down, you can only open the windows, which are also very small. 4. The bathroom is too small, the sink and toilet are crowded together, and they are located at the exit of the shower room. After washing for a while, the entire three areas are wet. 5. The hotel's hardware facilities are not very complete, such as no makeup mirrors, disposable razors, electric mosquito coils, etc.; 6. As mentioned earlier, the distance to Mizoguchi is about 4 kilometers. Although this distance is not far, it is not far away. The only problem with traffic in Jiuzhaigou Scenic Area is that there is only one single lane in both directions. After a slight flow of people, due to Jiuzhai characteristics such as traffic jams, taxi bargaining and no meters, it is very difficult to take a taxi. In addition, the construction of pedestrian paths in the scenic area is very difficult for walking. It's not friendly, especially on rainy days, so it's really inconvenient to go back and forth. The same goes for going to the bus station. And because the hotel is in the direction of Qianguqing, the shuttle bus from the scenic spot only goes to the county town, not to the direction of Qianguqing, which amplifies this shortcoming.
Second, in terms of software: 1. The Mizoguchi delivery service will not go directly to the visitor center. The delivery is more than two kilometers away. The remaining 12 kilometers still need to be walked by yourself. And when waiting in line for the bus the next day, the staff will not People are called in the order of arrival, but whoever is closest to the car rushes in first. Maybe this is the characteristic of Jiuzhaigou, and the transportation related to many scenic spots is also like this; 2. The hotel introduction says that it provides a taxi service. , in fact, there is only Mizoguchi service or airport pick-up (I did not verify the airport pick-up). If you want the hotel to help you call a taxi to pick you up or drop you off at the bus station for a fee, the staff will tell you that this service is not available, so no I know what this ride-hailing service is; 3. Service attitude. When asking normal questions, the tone of the staff seems to be very impatient; 4. There is no introduction about road meals, but I am still in the relevant The staff had to endure all kinds of impatient attitudes before asking about the relevant conditions.
Looking back carefully, this is the general feeling of this stay. I think if I rate it as 5 stars, it is indeed a bit worse than other places. I think the real star rating is between 3 and 4 stars or close to 4 stars, but Since there are too many flaws in this trip, I only gave it 3 stars this time for reference only.
